elementor-element-eeb9eaf elementor-column elementor-col-50 elementor-inner-column" data-element_type="column" data-id="eeb9eaf">\n<div class="elementor-column-wrap elementor-element-populated">\n<div class="elementor-widget-container">\n<div class="elementor-text-editor elementor-clearfix"><div style="text-align: left;"><p>ARION Coin, at it\xe2\x80\x99s heart, is a strong community-based coin. We created ARION together and are motivated by the drive and vision of the ARION project. Our aim is to help those communities where hyperinflation has left them with a highly devalued local currency. South America is a prime example at present.</p><p>Our main focus is targeting new and emerging markets where ARION can play a key role in integrating Cryptocurrency into everyday life.</p><p>ARION Masternodes are based on the DASH code and offer scalable, stable, reliable and secure transactions. The code is Open-source, peer 2 peer, decentralised and has functionality included like *Instantsend, Privatesend and *Dark Gravity Wave technology.</p><p><span style="letter-spacing: 0em;">With the help of a Well-known and Trusted Team, ARION was developed to be a High-End, High Value coin with a sustainable APR and long-term investment in mind.</span></p><p>Our goal is to use ARION as a payment solution. We want to make from going to your grocer, to buying your bread and milk, to buying a new car or home, a simple and effortless transaction. Aiming to make your \xe2\x80\x9cCrypto\xe2\x80\x9d integrate effortlessly into your everyday transactions, using QR code scanning technology and ARION debit cards to scan or swipe at all major retailers.</p></div></div>\n</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n</section>\n<section class="elementor-element elementor-element-733d9fd elementor-section-full_width class="elementor-widget-container">\n<div class="elementor-text-editor elementor-clearfix"><p style="font-weight: 400;">A cryptocurrency is a channel of exchange, which makes use of cryptography \xe2\x80\x93 (the art of writing or solving codes) to secure digital transactions and control creation of additional currency units. The development of cryptocurrency has been actively growing in the past decade, thus offering a broad range of transactional possibilities for both users and the crypto organizations.</p><p style="font-weight: 400;">Our aim is to build a formidable and stable digital currency platform whereby the distribution and value of the currency is not controlled solely by the miners, but by the community. Our purpose is to empower participants through the community dependent Marketing Channel, topping up projects and transactions. ARION COIN enables X11 miners to have something to mine, creating a better APR and higher return on investment on equipment that has not been performing well recently due to lower ROI. It is the objective of this project to inspire, and educate the community the need to have a formidable platform that is solely controlled by the community.</p></div>\n</div>\n</div>\n<div class="elementor-accordion-icon-closed fa fa-plus"></i>\n<i class="elementor-accordion-icon-opened fa fa-minus"></i>\n</span>\n<a href="">Q: What MUT can I Swap for Arion</a>\n</div>\n<div aria-labelledby="elementor-tab-title-2601" class="elementor-tab-content elementor-clearfix" data-tab="1" id="elementor-tab-content-2601" role="tabpanel"><p>You can only Swap the MUT you owned at the 120K Block<br> To see that Balance please look in the Mutual Channel under \xe2\x80\x9cWhat \xe2\x80\x93 block \xe2\x80\x93 are \xe2\x80\x93 we \xe2\x80\x93 on\xe2\x80\x9d to see the old explorer All other Masternodes will be purchased at the rate of what Arion is worth at the time of purchase on an exchange or at the pre-sale</p></div>\n</div>\n<div class="elementor-accordion-item">\n<div aria-controls="elementor-tab-content-2604" class="elementor-tab-title" data-tab="4" id="elementor-tab-title-2604" role="tab" tabindex="2604">\n<span aria-hidden="true" class="elementor-accordion-icon elementor-accordion-icon-left">\n<i class="elementor-accordion-icon-closed fa fa-plus"></i>\n<i class="elementor-accordion-icon-opened fa fa-minus"></i>\n</span>\n<a href="">Q: What happens if my coins are stuck at coinsmarkets?</a>\n</div>\n<div aria-labelledby="elementor-tab-title-2604" class="elementor-tab-content elementor-clearfix" data-tab="4" id="elementor-tab-content-2604" role="tabpanel"><p>All coins at coinsmarkets will be honoured when they come back and are not subject to the 28th February 2018 deadline.
